SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]

FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]

    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]

FROM [Books] AS [b]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]

    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]

FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

SELECT [b].[Id], [b].[Title], [b].[Author], [b].[ImageUrl], [b].[Genre], CASE
    WHEN NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Loans] AS [l]
        WHERE [b].[Id] = [l].[BookId] AND ([l].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END AS [IsAvailable], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l0].[LoanedOutTo]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l0]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l0].[BookId] AND ([l0].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [LoanedOutTo], (
    SELECT TOP(1) [l1].[DueDate]
    FROM [Loans] AS [l1]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = [l1].[BookId] AND ([l1].[ReturnedDate] IS NULL)) AS [DueDate]
FROM [Books] AS [b]
ORDER BY [b].[Title]

        FROM [Loans] AS [l]

    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
